< review>
I needed some time in an airplane that Santa Monica Flyers had in their fleet. They were professional in meeting my needs and communicated clearly when there were scheduling or weather issues.

All their staff is super friendly and knowledgeable. And they have a pretty sweet (and growing) fleet of airplanes.

I flew with Joseph, the general manager. I truly enjoyed flying with him and learning from him. Joseph and his staff take their jobs seriously but they make the experience fun. And flying should be fun! Either way, I highly recommend Santa Monica Flyers for those of you who may be in search of a flight school to conduct your primary or advanced training. They have a solid fleet and a lot of great instructors. They're not going to B.S. you like some of these other schools.

Regards,
An experienced instructor pilot< /review>

I ferried a Cessna 210 to SMO yesterday and had a friend who never flown in an airplane before, wanted to give him a quick ride around to motivate his dreams. I needed a headset, went in this place to rent one for him for an hour. An Old Lady approached me in a very negative way with her words. She told me to go purchase one from a store. They had about 10 headsets hanging on the wall. She refused to rent me one. Usually, aviation community are very friendly and helpful one to another one but not this place. I could not find a headset to rent or borrow around. Shame on that old lady. I am a CFI and a Ferry pilot. I have crossed the Country many times and never experienced such situation with an FBO or School. Her looks at me was definitely saying a lot of words more than " no they cant rent you one, you should purchase one". Hope you change your attitude towards pilots in this tight Aviation community. One positive attitude goes a long way.</Review>

< text>
Friendly at first, than you start to see the problems.

Here is what I found to be problematic.

1. Their rates seem low because they can offer the sport pilot program. If you look at becoming a private pilot their rates are very high. (ill explain why this is a problem)

2. Being a sport pilot ensures that you can only operate planes in that class, therefore you can only rent planes from santa monica flyers instead of flying Cessnas or Pipers which are everywhere.

3. These planes were down for maintenance all the time. Im not sure if it was because parts for these rare planes are hard to come by or because they need to be taken off the line often. For example they advertise having 5 planes available for a week I was training they were down to 1.

4. Santa Monica has frequently has a marine layer which goes right to the airport and inhibits you from flying VFR which  drags out the training.

(its hard to be proficient if you don't get to fly often because of maintenance and weather.)

5. If you want to fly at night, fly planes that are faster than your car, or continue your training as a pilot the sport pilot certificate is useless. Getting a private pilot certificate here is more expensive than all the other places I looked at.

All in all I wasted a lot of money here and ended up going to Van Nuys to complete my training.<//text>
<pics>None<//pics>< Response>

We have some of the lowest hourly rates on both our aircraft ($140/hr.) and our flight instructors ($75/hr.) in all of Southern California.  You can easily compare these rates by checking out flight school websites in the area.  What‚Äôs great is these Sportcruiser rates apply to both our Sport Pilot and Private Pilot training.  In fact, we offer a block rate, which lowers the aircraft rate to only $130 per hour!\n\n2.       Sport Pilots can fly any ‚ÄúLight Sport Aircraft‚Äù in the United States.  There are a number of places you can rent LSAs in Southern California, including Santa Monica, Torrance, Van Nuys, Camarillo and the Inland Empire.  Light Sport Aircraft were first certificated by the FAA in 2004 as a way of lowering the barriers to flying for those who didn‚Äôt want to spend as much time and money needed to obtain the Private Pilot Certificate.  An additional advantage to flying Light Sport Aircraft is, not only can they fly as high as any other light, single piston airplane and almost as fast (120 mph as the crow flies), but they also burn half as much fuel, cutting the carbon footprint of your flight in half.  You can easily get to Santa Barbara, San Diego or Riverside from Santa Monica in as little as 45 minutes, have dinner and be back before Sunset!\n\n3.       Santa Monica Flyers has a solid reputation for extremely safe aircraft operations and training.  We immediately ground our aircraft if even something very small isn‚Äôt working right.  This is one area that distinguishes us from many flight schools in the area. You‚Äôre right, maintenance, and weather can get in the way of flight training ‚Äì and often does ‚Äì regardless of which flight school you train at.  The question is, what kinds of decisions does your flight school make about maintenance on the aircraft you train in?\n\n4. I wanted to get this issue fixed ASAP, but because they were moving offices they could not see my daughter until a week out from when I was calling because I was seeking for my insurance to cover the procedure and visit. I called ahead of time asking for specific charges. I did not want to pay 650$ for this when I have insurance that would cover it. I did have a pediatrician and an ENT office that would cover the procedure, not even a co-pay. I went to her because she was recommended and they confirmed on the phone before I was in the office that I had insurance and yes it would be covered 100%. The day of the procedure came and it was not until after the procedure that it was brought to my attention that my daughter was not covered and I would have to pay out of pocket and submit a "superbill." I did not appreciate this, but they assured me I would be reimbursed. This all occurred the last week of March, it is now June. I only received a small partial reimbursement from my insurance and was explained by them that they should not have charged me that much and I was to get the rest from the office. I had faith that this office would stand by their word and good name to give me back my money they said would be reimbursed. They admitted they were in the wrong and it should have been handled differently, but still will not reimburse me. This is just one of my issues with this office. This is very unprofessional! Now, this is all on her ways of handling business, as for her procedures. I have yet to see any problems with what was altered in my child's mouth. I have to say she did a good job and I feel it was the best route to take when having this done. She did not seem to be in pain, which was my personal goal with her. I really wish I could say I would come back here and recommend her to others, but I do not and will not for the purpose that I am still out 400$ of my own money when I have insurance that could have covered this.
